## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p07/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 32768
K = 64
N = 32768
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
BLOCK_K = 16
WAVE_M = 32
WAVE_N = 32
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    warp_id = tid // 64
    warp_row = warp_id // 2
    warp_col = warp_id % 2
    block_row = S.block_id(1)
    block_col = S.block_id(0)

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

    a_words = S.make_shared((512,), S.u32)
    b_words = S.make_shared((512,), S.u32)
    a_lane_packs = S.view(a_words, S.u32, S.make_layout((128, 4), (4, 1)))
    b_lane_packs = S.view(b_words, S.u32, S.make_layout((128, 4), (4, 1)))
    b_lane_vals = S.view(b_words, S.bf16, S.make_layout((128, 8), (8, 1)))
    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    block_row_base = block_row * BLOCK_M
    block_col_base = block_col * BLOCK_N
    warp_row_base = warp_row * WAVE_M
    warp_col_base = warp_col * WAVE_N

    for ko in S.range(K // BLOCK_K):
        if tid < 128:
            a_linear = tid * 8
            a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
            a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
            a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
            load_group = tid % 2
            lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
            lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
            a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
            a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
            a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
            a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
        else:
            b_tid = tid - 128
            b_linear = b_tid * 8
            b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
            b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
            b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
            b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            row_mod8 = b_row % 8
            row_half = row_mod8 // 4
            if b_row < 8:
                row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
                for e in S.range(4):
                    pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
                    pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
            else:
                row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
                for e in S.range(4):
                    pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
                    pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
        a_half = lane // 32
        b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)

        a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
        b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
        a_vec = S.view(a_lane_packs[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_vec = S.view(b_lane_packs[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    out_col = block_col_base + warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
    out_row_base = block_row_base + warp_row_base + 4 * (lane // 32)
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        out_row = out_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
        C[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx], S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A, B):
        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
            raise ValueError(f"Expected A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise ValueError(f"Expected bf16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}")

        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 32768
K = 64
N = 32768
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
BLOCK_K = 16
WAVE_M = 32
WAVE_N = 32
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    warp_id = tid // 64
    warp_row = warp_id // 2
    warp_col = warp_id % 2
    block_row = S.block_id(1)
    block_col = S.block_id(0)

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

    a_words = S.make_shared((512,), S.u32)
    b_words = S.make_shared((512,), S.u32)
    a_lane_packs = S.view(a_words, S.u32, S.make_layout((128, 4), (4, 1)))
    b_lane_packs = S.view(b_words, S.u32, S.make_layout((128, 4), (4, 1)))
    b_lane_vals = S.view(b_words, S.bf16, S.make_layout((128, 8), (8, 1)))
    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    block_row_base = block_row * BLOCK_M
    block_col_base = block_col * BLOCK_N
    warp_row_base = warp_row * WAVE_M
    warp_col_base = warp_col * WAVE_N

    for ko in S.range(K // BLOCK_K):
        if tid < 128:
            a_linear = tid * 8
            a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
            a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
            a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
            load_group = tid % 2
            lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
            lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
            a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
            a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
            a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
            a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
        else:
            b_tid = tid - 128
            b_linear = b_tid * 8
            b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
            b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
            b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
            b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            row_mod8 = b_row % 8
            row_half = row_mod8 // 4
            if b_row < 8:
                row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
                for e in S.range(4):
                    pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
                    pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
            else:
                row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
                for e in S.range(4):
                    pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
                    pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
                    b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
        a_half = lane // 32
        b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)

        a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
        b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
        a_vec = S.view(a_lane_packs[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+def load_ab_stage(
+    tid,
+    block_row_base,
+    block_col_base,

+    b_rsrc,

+    if tid < 128:
+        a_linear = tid * 8
+        a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
+        a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
+        a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        load_group = tid % 2
+        lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
+    else:
+        b_tid = tid - 128
+        b_linear = b_tid * 8
+        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+        b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        row_mod8 = b_row % 8
+        row_half = row_mod8 // 4
+        if b_row < 8:
+            row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+        else:
+            row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+
+
+def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs):
+    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
+    a_half = lane // 32
+    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
+
+    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
+    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
+    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_idx]
+    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_idx]
+    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
+    return acc
+
+
 @substrate.jit

     A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),

 THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
 A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
 B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+K_TILES = K // BLOCK_K
 
 
+def load_ab_stage(
+    tid,
+    block_row_base,
+    block_col_base,
+    ko,
+    a_rsrc,
+    b_rsrc,
+    zero,
+    a_words,
+    b_words,
+    b_lane_vals,
+):
+    if tid < 128:
+        a_linear = tid * 8
+        a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
+        a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
+        a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        load_group = tid % 2
+        lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
+    else:
+        b_tid = tid - 128
+        b_linear = b_tid * 8
+        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+        b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        row_mod8 = b_row % 8
+        row_half = row_mod8 // 4
+        if b_row < 8:
+            row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+        else:
+            row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+
+
+def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs):
+    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
+    a_half = lane // 32
+    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
+
+    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
+    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
+    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_idx]
+    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_idx]
+    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
+    return acc
+
+

index c51767b57467ac8945f194b067412e73ab93da09..22f6bf5a4d77cd2605f4941e5c77456b9de95891
--- a/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p07/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py
+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p07/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py
@@ -17,9 +17,79 @@
 THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
 A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
 B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+K_TILES = K // BLOCK_K
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def load_ab_stage(
+    tid,
+    block_row_base,
+    block_col_base,
+    ko,
+    a_rsrc,
+    b_rsrc,
+    zero,
+    a_words,
+    b_words,
+    b_lane_vals,
+):
+    if tid < 128:
+        a_linear = tid * 8
+        a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
+        a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
+        a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        load_group = tid % 2
+        lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
+    else:
+        b_tid = tid - 128
+        b_linear = b_tid * 8
+        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+        b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        row_mod8 = b_row % 8
+        row_half = row_mod8 // 4
+        if b_row < 8:
+            row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+        else:
+            row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
 
 
 @substrate.jit
+def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs):
+    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
+    a_half = lane // 32
+    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
+
+    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
+    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
+    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_idx]
+    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_idx]
+    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
+    return acc
+
+
+@substrate.jit
 def gemm_kernel(
     A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
     B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16),
@@ -37,11 +107,11 @@

+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)

+        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
+        a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
+        a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]

+        b_linear = b_tid * 8
+        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N

+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)

 @substrate.jit
+def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs):
+    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
+    a_half = lane // 32
+    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
+
+    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
+    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
+    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_idx]
+    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_idx]
+    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
+    return acc

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 32768
K = 64
N = 32768
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
BLOCK_K = 16
WAVE_M = 32
WAVE_N = 32
WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
K_TILES = K // BLOCK_K


@substrate.jit
def load_ab_stage(
    tid,
    block_row_base,
    block_col_base,
    ko,
    a_rsrc,
    b_rsrc,
    zero,
    a_words,
    b_words,
    b_lane_vals,
):
    if tid < 128:
        a_linear = tid * 8
        a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
        a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
        a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
        load_group = tid % 2
        lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
        a_words[lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
        a_words[lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
        a_words[lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
        a_words[lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
    else:
        b_tid = tid - 128
        b_linear = b_tid * 8
        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
        b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
        b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        row_mod8 = b_row % 8
        row_half = row_mod8 // 4
        if b_row < 8:
            row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
            for e in S.range(4):
                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
        else:
            row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
            for e in S.range(4):
                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
                b_lane_vals[pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
                b_lane_vals[pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]


@substrate.jit
def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs):
    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
    a_half = lane // 32
    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)

    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_idx]
    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_idx]
    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
    return acc


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % 64
    warp_id = tid // 64
    warp_row = warp_id // 2
    warp_col = warp_id % 2
    block_row = S.block_id(1)
    block_col = S.block_id(0)

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)

    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 512), S.u32)
    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 512), S.u32)
    a_lane_packs = S.view(a_words, S.u32, S.make_layout((2, 128, 4), (512, 4, 1)))
    b_lane_packs = S.view(b_words, S.u32, S.make_layout((2, 128, 4), (512, 4, 1)))
    b_lane_vals = S.view(b_words, S.bf16, S.make_layout((2, 128, 8), (1024, 8, 1)))
    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    block_row_base = block_row * BLOCK_M
    block_col_base = block_col * BLOCK_N
    warp_row_base = warp_row * WAVE_M
    warp_col_base = warp_col * WAVE_N

    load_ab_stage(
        tid, block_row_base, block_col_base, 0, a_rsrc, b_rsrc, zero, a_words[0], b_words[0], b_lane_vals[0]
    )
    S.syncthreads()

    for ko_pair in S.range(K_TILES // 2):
        base_ko = ko_pair * 2
        next_stage = 1
        load_ab_stage(
            tid,
            block_row_base,
            block_col_base,
            base_ko + 1,
            a_rsrc,
            b_rsrc,
            zero,
            a_words[next_stage],
            b_words[next_stage],
            b_lane_vals[next_stage],
        )
        acc = mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs[0], b_lane_packs[0])
        S.syncthreads()

        if ko_pair + 1 < (K_TILES // 2):
            load_ab_stage(
                tid,
                block_row_base,
                block_col_base,
                base_ko + 2,
                a_rsrc,
                b_rsrc,
                zero,
                a_words[0],
                b_words[0],
                b_lane_vals[0],
            )
        acc = mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs[1], b_lane_packs[1])
        S.syncthreads()

    out_col = block_col_base + warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
    out_row_base = block_row_base + warp_row_base + 4 * (lane // 32)
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        out_row = out_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + (acc_idx % 4)
        C[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx], S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A, B):
        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
            raise ValueError(f"Expected A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise ValueError(f"Expected bf16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}")

        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

+    return acc

codex
The crash is likely from the staged shared-memory views rather than the pipeline structure itself. I’m flattening the LDS buffers and using explicit stage base offsets, which is the simplest safe version of the same schedule.
apply patch

@@ -17,6 +17,78 @@
 THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
 A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
 B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+K_TILES = K // BLOCK_K
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def load_ab_stage(
+    tid,
+    block_row_base,
+    block_col_base,
+    ko,
+    a_rsrc,
+    b_rsrc,
+    zero,
+    a_words,
+    b_words,
+    b_lane_vals,
+    a_stage_base,
+    b_stage_base,
+):
+    if tid < 128:
+        a_linear = tid * 8
+        a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
+        a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
+        a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        load_group = tid % 2
+        lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
+    else:
+        b_tid = tid - 128
+        b_linear = b_tid * 8
+        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+        b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        row_mod8 = b_row % 8
+        row_half = row_mod8 // 4
+        if b_row < 8:
+            row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+        else:
+            row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs, a_stage_base, b_stage_base):
+    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
+    a_half = lane // 32
+    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
+
+    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
+    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
+    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_stage_base + a_idx]
+    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_stage_base + b_idx]
+    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
+    return acc

--- a/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p07/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py
+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p07/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py
@@ -17,6 +17,78 @@
 THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 64 * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
 A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
 B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+K_TILES = K // BLOCK_K
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def load_ab_stage(
+    tid,
+    block_row_base,
+    block_col_base,
+    ko,
+    a_rsrc,
+    b_rsrc,
+    zero,
+    a_words,
+    b_words,
+    b_lane_vals,
+    a_stage_base,
+    b_stage_base,
+):
+    if tid < 128:
+        a_linear = tid * 8
+        a_row = a_linear // BLOCK_K
+        a_col = a_linear % BLOCK_K
+        a_offset = ((block_row_base + a_row) * K + ko * BLOCK_K + a_col) * 2
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        load_group = tid % 2
+        lane_base0 = (a_row * 2 + 0) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        lane_base1 = (a_row * 2 + 1) * 4 + load_group * 2
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base0 + 0] = a_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base0 + 1] = a_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base1 + 0] = a_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_stage_base + lane_base1 + 1] = a_pack[3]
+    else:
+        b_tid = tid - 128
+        b_linear = b_tid * 8
+        b_row = b_linear // BLOCK_N
+        b_col = b_linear % BLOCK_N
+        b_offset = ((ko * BLOCK_K + b_row) * N + block_col_base + b_col) * 2
+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset, S.i32), 0)
+        b_vals = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        row_mod8 = b_row % 8
+        row_half = row_mod8 // 4
+        if b_row < 8:
+            row_slot = row_mod8 % 4
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+        else:
+            row_slot = 4 + (row_mod8 % 4)
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                pack_idx0 = (b_col + e) * 2 + row_half
+                pack_idx1 = (b_col + 4 + e) * 2 + row_half
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx0, row_slot] = b_vals[0, e, 0]
+                b_lane_vals[b_stage_base + pack_idx1, row_slot] = b_vals[1, e, 0]
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_stage(acc, warp_row_base, warp_col_base, lane, a_lane_packs, b_lane_packs, a_stage_base, b_stage_base):
+    a_row = warp_row_base + (lane % 32)
+    a_half = lane // 32
+    b_col = warp_col_base + (lane % 32)
+
+    a_idx = a_row * 2 + a_half
+    b_idx = b_col * 2 + a_half
+    a_pack = a_lane_packs[a_stage_base + a_idx]
+    b_pack = b_lane_packs[b_stage_base + b_idx]
+    a_vec = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    b_vec = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[0], b_vec[0], acc)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_vec[1], b_vec[1], acc)
+    return acc

codex
I’m removing the remaining abstraction around the hot loop and writing the four K-tiles explicitly. `K` is fixed here, so a manual unroll is the fastest path to a stable, executable pipelined version.

codex
Implemented the optimized kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p07/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py). I left `candidate_input.py` unchanged.

The kernel keeps the 4-wave MFMA structure and adds a double-buffered LDS layout with an explicitly unrolled 4-tile K schedule, loading the next tile into the alternate LDS stage before consuming the current one. Validation passed with the required command: correctness `true`, compiled `true`, candidate runtime about `7.08 us` on the recorded run.
